If you don't know what that means, then you probably haven't used the pngfix script, and this comment may be ignored :) */

For older browsers, a default of 'black' is given before this rule. Guideline to support older browsers: if you haven't already declared a border-color for an element, be sure to do so, e.g. when you first declare the border-width. */

      var $fbra_deliveryDates = $('#fbra_checkoutDeliverySummary > div > div > div > div > .fbra_deliveryDate');

      var rexDelivery = new RegExp(/ \d\d:\d\d a \d\d:\d\d/);



      $fbra_deliveryDates.each(function(index){

           var dateText = $(this).text();

           if( rexDelivery.test(dateText) ) {

            }

            else if( dateText.indexOf(' entre') !== -1 ) {

      });

  <script>_satellite["_runScript2"](function(event, target, Promise) {

if(/conf/i.test(document.URL) && (_satellite.getVar('ecom_orderId')||_satellite.getVar('ecom_purchaseID'))){

		syteDataLayer = window.syteDataLayer || [];

		syteDataLayer.push({

            id:_satellite.getVar('ecom_orderId')||_satellite.getVar('ecom_purchaseID'),

			value: getTotal(),

		});

function getProd() {

	var prodsArr = []

	digitalData.ecom.productList.forEach(function (el) {

		var tempObj = {

			'sku': el.sku,

			'price': el.price,

			'quantity': el.quantity

		};

		prodsArr.push(tempObj);

	});

	return prodsArr;

}



function getTotal() {

	var total = 0;

	digitalData.ecom.productList.forEach(function (el) {

		total = el.price + total;

	})

	return total;

}

  <script>_satellite["_runScript6"](function(event, target, Promise) {

function highlightDeliveryToday() {

    var firstCalendarCell = document.querySelector(".fbra_dateTimeDelivery__daySlotsColumn").querySelector(".fbra_dateTimeDeliveryColumn__calendarDate");

    if (firstCalendarCell) {

        var clientTodayDate = new Date().getDate();

        var checkoutFirstDate = firstCalendarCell.innerText.match(/\d+/);

        if (checkoutFirstDate && parseInt(checkoutFirstDate[0]) === clientTodayDate) {

            firstCalendarCell.innerText = "Hoy";

            var dateColumn = firstCalendarCell.closest(".fbra_dateTimeDeliveryColumn");

            var arraySlots = dateColumn.querySelectorAll(".fbra_dateTimeDeliverySlot");

            firstCalendarCell.classList.add("sameDayTitle");

            arraySlots.forEach(function(el){

                el.classList.add("sameDaySlot");



            }

            );

        } else if(firstCalendarCell.innerText !== "Hoy"){

            firstCalendarCell.classList.remove("sameDayTitle");

        }

    }

}



function highlightDeliveryTodayMobile() {

    var firstCalendarCell = document.querySelector(".fbra_dateTimeDelivery__daySlotsColumnMobile").querySelector(".fbra_dateTimeDelivery__calendarDate");

    if (firstCalendarCell) {



        var clientTodayDate = new Date().getDate();

        var checkoutFirstDate = firstCalendarCell.innerText.match(/\d+/);

        if (checkoutFirstDate && parseInt(checkoutFirstDate[0]) === clientTodayDate) {

            firstCalendarCell.innerText = "Hoy";

            var dateColumn = firstCalendarCell.closest(".fbra_dateTimeDelivery__mobileDaySlotsColumnContainer");

            var dayArraySlots = dateColumn.querySelectorAll(".fbra_dateTimeDeliverySlot");

            var hourArraySlots = dateColumn.querySelectorAll(".fbra_dateTimeDeliverySlot__slotTimeRange");

            firstCalendarCell.classList.add("sameDayTitle");

            dayArraySlots.forEach(function(el){

                el.classList.add("sameDaySlot");

            }

            );



            hourArraySlots.forEach(function(el){

                el.classList.add("sameHourSlot");

            }

            );

        } else if(firstCalendarCell.innerText !== "Hoy"){

            firstCalendarCell.classList.remove("sameDayTitle");

        }

    }

}



function highlightWrapper() {

    if (document.querySelector(".fbra_whenToDeliver__shippingMethodBody")) {

        highlightDeliveryToday();

        highlightDeliveryTodayMobile();

    }

}



var checkingInterval = setInterval(highlightWrapper, 50);

  base: function base() {

    var newclass = arguments.length > 0 && arguments[0] !== undefined ? arguments[0] : '';

    var create = document.createElement('div');

    create.className = 'tooltip__container' + newclass;

    create.innerHTML = this.innerTooltip();

    return create;

  },

  innerTooltip: function innerTooltip() {

    return "\n            <div class=\"tooltip__content\">\n                <p class=\"tooltip__title\">\xBFNo sabes cu\xE1l es tu zona?</p>\n            </div>\n            <div class=\"tooltip__popup-container tt-hide\">\n                <div class=\"tooltip__popup-content\">\n                    <p class=\"tooltip__paragraph\">Si est\xE1s en Bogota puedes elegir estas dos Zonas de despacho.</p>\n                    <ul class=\"tooltip__list\">\n                        <li class=\"tooltip__list-item\"><strong>Zona Norte:</strong> De la calle 80 hacia el Norte.</li> \n                        <li class=\"tooltip__list-item\"><strong>Zona Sur:</strong> De la calle 80 hacia el Sur.</li> \n                    </ul>\n          <p class=\"tooltip__paragraph\">Las entregas con envíos Express serán mayor de 3 horas para las localidades de Usme y San Cristóbal.</p>\n      </div>\n            </div>\n        ";

  }

};

var tool = {

  checkForElement: function checkForElement(element, callback) {

    var el = element;

    var interval = setInterval(function (e) {

      var theElement = document.getElementById(el) || document.querySelectorAll(el);

      if (theElement.length === 0 || theElement === null) return;

      callback();

      clearInterval(interval);

    }, 400);

  }

};

var ui = {

  insertTooltip: function insertTooltip() {

    var labelBarrio = document.querySelector('.fbra_formItem__comuna:not(select) label');

    var labelBarrioM = document.querySelector('.fbra_formItem__comuna:not(select)');

    var windowInner = window.innerWidth;

    var checkMobile = windowInner < 570 ? ' tooltip__mobile' : '';



    if (windowInner < 570) {

      labelBarrioM.appendChild(template.base(checkMobile));

      if (!document.querySelector('.tooltip__container')) return;

      this.clickOnIt();

    } else {

      labelBarrio.appendChild(template.base());

      if (!document.querySelector('.tooltip__container')) return;

      this.hoverIt();

    }

  },

  hoverIt: function hoverIt() {

    var toHover = document.querySelector('.tooltip__container');

    var elementToAddClass = document.querySelector('.tooltip__popup-container');

    toHover.addEventListener('mouseenter', function () {

      elementToAddClass.classList.add('tt-show');

    });

    toHover.addEventListener('mouseleave', function () {

      elementToAddClass.classList.remove('tt-show');

    });

  },

  clickOnIt: function clickOnIt() {

    var toClickOn = document.querySelector('.tooltip__container.tooltip__mobile');

    var elementToAddClass = document.querySelector('.tooltip__mobile .tooltip__popup-container');

    window.addEventListener('click', function (e) {

      var classNameTooltip = e.target.className;



      if (!/popup-container/.test(classNameTooltip)) {

        if (/tt-show/.test(elementToAddClass.classList)) {

          elementToAddClass.classList.remove('tt-show');

        }

      }



      if (document.querySelector('.tooltip__mobile' + ' .' + classNameTooltip)) {

        if (!/tt-show/.test(elementToAddClass.classList)) {

          elementToAddClass.classList.add('tt-show');

        }

      }

    });

  }

};



(function () {

  tool.checkForElement('comuna', function () {

    if (document.querySelector('.tooltip__container')) return;

    ui.insertTooltip();

  });

})();

});</script>

  <script>_satellite["_runScript12"](function(event, target, Promise) {

function checkJota(int) {



    var jotaObject = {};

    digitalData.ecom.productList.forEach(function(el) {

        var jota = el.backendCategory.slice(0, int);

        if (jotaObject[jota] === undefined) {

            jotaObject[jota] = el.price * el.quantity;

        } else {

            jotaObject[jota] = jotaObject[jota] + (el.price * el.quantity);

        }

    });



    var finalJota;

    Object.keys(jotaObject).forEach(function(el) {

        if (finalJota === undefined) {

            finalJota = el;

        } else {

 

            finalJota = jotaObject[finalJota] > jotaObject[el] ? finalJota : el;



        }



    });

    return finalJota;



}

var checkoutLinea;

var checkoutSublinea;

if (digitalData.ecom && digitalData.ecom.productList && digitalData.ecom.productList[0] && digitalData.ecom.productList[0].backendCategory) {

    checkoutLinea = checkJota(3);

    checkoutSublinea = checkJota(5);

} else {

    checkoutLinea = null;

    checkoutSublinea = null;

}





var appmedallia="web";

if(_satellite.cookie.get('dtm_appmedallia')){

  appmedallia="app";

}

var newObject ={

        'no_show': _satellite.getVar('noShow'),

        'app':appmedallia,

        'j_linea':checkoutLinea,

        'j_sublinea':checkoutSublinea

    };





digitalData.medalliaParameters = newObject;

});</script>
